' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function DEF0631() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		Dim stringBuilder As StringBuilder = New StringBuilder()
		Dim stringBuilder2 As StringBuilder = stringBuilder
		stringBuilder2.Append("UPDATE T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO                                            ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("SET DELETE_FLG = '1'                                                   ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("WHERE  SEIKYU_YM       = '{0}'                                         ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("AND    (                                                               ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("              (MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = '{1}' AND SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = '{2}')    ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("           OR (MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = '{2}' AND SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = '{1}')    ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("       )                                                               ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("AND    HIYOKOMOKU_CD  IN ('{3}','{4}')                                   ").Append(vbCrLf)
		stringBuilder2.Append("AND    UKETSUKE_NO     = '{4}'                                         ").Append(vbCrLf)
		result = stringBuilder.ToString()
	Catch expr_DD As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_DD)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_DD
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

Public Function SCF0023() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try

	Try
		result = "SELECT KOBAIHIN.SOSHIKI_CD,                  KOBAIHIN.KOBAI_CD,                  KOBAIHIN.GAIBU_GYOSHA_CD,                  GYOSHA.GYOSHA_RYAKU_MEI,               KOBAIHIN.KOBAI_SURYO_TANI,                  M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,                  KOBAIHIN.SHIIRE_TANKA_GK,                  KOBAIHIN.SHIIRESAKI_MAIL_ADRS,               KOBAIHIN.HANBAI_MATOME_GK,                  KOBAIHIN.SONOTA_KINGAKU_MEI,                  KOBAIHIN.SONITA_KINGAKU_GK,                  KOBAIHIN.HANBAI_TESURYO_RT,                  KOBAIHIN.JISHA_KOBAI_CD,                  KOBAIHIN.REMARKS,                  KOBAIHIN.UPDATE_DT,                  KOBAIHIN.UPDATE_TNT_ID,                  KOBAIHIN.GAMEN_ID, KOBAIHIN.KOBAI_MEI LIKE '{3}%'  " & vbTab & vbTab & "         AND KOBAIHIN.TASOSHIKI_KOBAI_CD = ''                  AND KOBAIHIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD                  AND M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD                  AND KOBAIHIN.KOBAI_CD *= TA_KOBAIHIN.TASOSHIKI_KOBAI_CD                AND KOBAIHIN.GAIBU_GYOSHA_CD *= GYOSHA.GYOSHA_CD                AND GYOSHA.GYOSHA_KBN = '2' ORDER BY KOBAIHIN.KOBAI_CD"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function SCF0510() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = " SELECT max(MAIN2.KENSU) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & "MAIN2.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.GYOSHA_MEI,                 MAIN2.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_TANKA) as URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_NEBIKI) as URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) as URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK) as URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.BIKO,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   " & vbTab & "FROM(    SELECT DISTINCT" & vbTab & "MAIN.KENSU,           " & vbTab & "MAIN.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.GYOSHA_MEI,                 MAIN.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.BIKO,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI    FROM(SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                C.HACHU_DT, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK, " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM, " & vbTab & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'  AND    JYOBU.JYOBU_SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'  AND    C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD   AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{1}%'   AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'   AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD GROUP BY         C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,         C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN UNION ALL   SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                C.HACHU_DT, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK, " & vbTab & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK, " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO, " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM, " & vbTab & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'  AND    JYOBU.JYOBU_SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'  AND    C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD   AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{1}%'   AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'   AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD GROUP BY         C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,         C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,  " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN UNION ALL   SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                 C.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.JYOBU_URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.JYOBU_URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO,   " & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'    AND    JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'    AND    LEFT(C.GYOSHA_CD,5) = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD   AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{1}%'  AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'    AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD   GROUP BY          C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,          C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,          C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN  ) MAIN  ) MAIN2  WHERE MAIN2.URIAGE_TANKA IS NOT NULL    GROUP BY          MAIN2.HACHU_NO, MAIN2.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, MAIN2.GYOSHA_CD, MAIN2.GYOSHA_MEI,          MAIN2.HACHU_DT, MAIN2.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_CD,          MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_MEI, MAIN2.SEISAN_YM, MAIN2.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,MAIN2.KAKUTEI_KBN,MAIN2.BIKO        ORDER BY MAIN2.HACHU_NO  "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

		result = " SELECT max(MAIN2.KENSU) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & "MAIN2.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN2.GYOSHA_MEI,                 MAIN2.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_TANKA) as URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_NEBIKI) as URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) as URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "max(MAIN2.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK) as URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.BIKO,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "MAIN2.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   " & vbTab & "FROM(    SELECT DISTINCT" & vbTab & "MAIN.KENSU,           " & vbTab & "MAIN.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN.GYOSHA_MEI,                 MAIN.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.BIKO,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "MAIN.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI    FROM(SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                 C.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO,   " & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'    AND   JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'  AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD  AND   C.HACHU_NO LIKE '{1}%'    AND   C.HACHU_DT >=  '{2}'    AND   C.HACHU_DT <=  '{3}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT >=  '{4}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT <=  '{5}'    AND   C.GYOSHA_CD LIKE '{6}%'    AND   C.KOBAI_CD LIKE '{7}%'    AND   C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN LIKE '{8}%'   AND   C.NOHINSAKI_CD LIKE '{9}%'    AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{10}%'    AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'    AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD   GROUP BY          C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,          C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,          C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN  UNION ALL   SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                 C.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO,   " & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'    AND   JYOBU.JYOBU_SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'  AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD  AND   C.HACHU_NO LIKE '{1}%'    AND   C.HACHU_DT >=  '{2}'    AND   C.HACHU_DT <=  '{3}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT >=  '{4}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT <=  '{5}'    AND   C.GYOSHA_CD LIKE '{6}%'    AND   C.KOBAI_CD LIKE '{7}%'    AND   C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN LIKE '{8}%'   AND   C.NOHINSAKI_CD LIKE '{9}%'    AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{10}%'    AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'    AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD   GROUP BY          C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,          C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,          C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN  UNION ALL   SELECT " & vbTab & "count(C.HACHU_NO) as KENSU,           " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.HACHU_NO,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_CD,   " & vbTab & vbTab & "C.GYOSHA_MEI,                 C.HACHU_DT,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_CD,   " & vbTab & "C.NOHINSAKI_MEI,   " & vbTab & "C.KAKUTEI_KBN,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_TANKA) AS URIAGE_TANKA,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_NEBIKI,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK) AS URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "SUM(C.JYOBU_URIAGE_GOKEI_GK + C.JYOBU_URIAGE_SHOHIZEI_GK - C.JYOBU_URIAGE_NEBIKI) AS URIAGE_GOKEI_GK,   " & vbTab & "MAX(C.BIKO) AS BIKO,   " & vbTab & "C.SEISAN_YM,   " & vbTab & "ISNULL(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI   FROM    T_SHIZAI_HACHU AS C,M_SOSHIKI,M_SOSHIKI AS JYOBU   WHERE   C.DELETE_FLG != '1'    AND   JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD = '{0}'    AND   LEFT(C.GYOSHA_CD,5) = JYOBU.SOSHIKI_CD  AND   C.HACHU_NO LIKE '{1}%'    AND   C.HACHU_DT >=  '{2}'    AND   C.HACHU_DT <=  '{3}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT >=  '{4}'    AND   C.NOHIN_DT <=  '{5}'    AND   C.GYOSHA_CD LIKE '{6}%'    AND   C.KOBAI_CD LIKE '{7}%'    AND   C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN LIKE '{8}%'   AND   C.NOHINSAKI_CD LIKE '{9}%'    AND   C.SEISAN_YM LIKE '{10}%'    AND   C.GAIBU_NAIBU_KBN = '2'    AND   C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD   GROUP BY          C.HACHU_NO, C.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, C.GYOSHA_CD, C.GYOSHA_MEI,          C.HACHU_DT, C.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, C.NOHINSAKI_CD,          C.NOHINSAKI_MEI, C.SEISAN_YM, M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,C.KAKUTEI_KBN ) MAIN ) MAIN2  WHERE MAIN2.URIAGE_TANKA IS NOT NULL    GROUP BY          MAIN2.HACHU_NO, MAIN2.SEIKYUMOTO_CD, MAIN2.GYOSHA_CD, MAIN2.GYOSHA_MEI,          MAIN2.HACHU_DT, MAIN2.NOHIN_JYOTAI_KBN, MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_CD,          MAIN2.NOHINSAKI_MEI, MAIN2.SEISAN_YM, MAIN2.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,MAIN2.KAKUTEI_KBN,MAIN2.BIKO        ORDER BY MAIN2.HACHU_NO  "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = JUCHU.UKETSUKE_NO))   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD  UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS HACHU.NEBIKI AS ZEINUKI_GK,  HACHU.SHOHIZEI_GK AS SHOHIZEI_GK,  HACHU.UKETSUKE_DT AS HASEI_DT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '2' AS SEQ_NO FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_HACHU AS HACHU,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '3'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = HACHU.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = HACHU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = HACHU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = HACHU.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  CRT.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK AS ZEINUKI_GK,  '0' AS SHOHIZEI_GK,  CRT.HASEI_DT AS HASEI_DT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '3' AS SEQ_NO  FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO AS CRT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = CRT.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = CRT.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO <> CRT.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  CRT.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK AS ZEINUKI_GK,  '0' AS SHOHIZEI_GK,  CRT.HASEI_DT AS HASEI_DT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '4' AS SEQ_NO  FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO AS CRT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = CRT.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = CRT.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD, = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = KBT.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = KBT.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD, T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = TEIGAKU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = TEIGAKU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = TEIGAKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_GK > 0   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  SONOTA.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK AS ZEINUKI_GK,  '0' AS SHOHIZEI_GK,  SONOTA.HASEI_DT AS HASEI_DT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '7' AS SEQ_NO  FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU AS SONOTA,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = SONOTA.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = SONOTA.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = SONOTA.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = SONOTA.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD ) AS MAIN   WHERE MAIN.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1'   ORDER BY MAIN.SEIKYU_YM,   MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,   SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,   SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,   HIYOKOMOKU_CD,   ZEINUKI_GK,   SHOHIZEI_GK "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = CRT.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO <> CRT.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  SUM(CRT.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK) AS GOUKEI,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '4' AS SEQ_NO  FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO AS CRT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = CRT.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = CRT.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = CRT.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = CRT.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  SUM(KBT.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK) AS GOUKEI,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '5' AS SEQ_NO FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_KBT_TESURYO AS KBT,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = KBT.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = KBT.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = KBT.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = KBT.UKETSUKE_NO   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  SUM(TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_GK + TEIGAKU.SHOHIZEI_GK) AS GOUKEI,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '6' AS SEQ_NO FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU AS TEIGAKU,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = TEIGAKU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = TEIGAKU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = TEIGAKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_GK > 0   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD UNION ALL SELECT  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN,  SUM(SONOTA.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK) AS GOUKEI,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,  MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,  '7' AS SEQ_NO  FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,  T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU AS SONOTA,  M_HIYO_KOMOKU,  M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,  M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'  AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '1'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = SONOTA.SEIKYU_YM   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = SONOTA.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = SONOTA.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = SONOTA.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD   AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD ) AS MAIN    GROUP BY MAIN.SEIKYU_YM,   MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,   SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,   SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,   MEISAI_KBN,   HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,   MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,   SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,   ORDER BY MAIN.SEIKYU_YM,   MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,   SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,   SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,   HIYOKOMOKU_CD,   GOUKEI "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function SEF0190() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "SELECT H.SEIKYU_YM,        H.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,        H.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,        H.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,        H.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,        H.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK AS GOKEI_GK,        M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,        M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,        '1' AS KENSU  FROM T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU AS H,M_HIYO_KOMOKU,M_SOSHIKI   WHERE H.SEIKYU_YM >= '{0}' AND H.SEIKYU_YM <= '{1}'   AND  H.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{2}%'   AND  H.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{3}%'   AND  H.HIYOKOMOKU_CD LIKE '{4}%'   AND  H.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1'   AND  H.DELETE_FLG != '1'   AND  H.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD   AND  H.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD  ORDER BY  H.SEIKYU_YM,H.HIYOKOMOKU_CD"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception

		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try

End Function

' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function SEF0191() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "SELECT MAIN.SEIKYU_YM, MAIN.HIYOKOMOKU_CD, M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI, MAIN.KENSU, MAIN.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,     CASE  WHEN MAIN.KENSU <= 1 THEN M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI     ELSE  M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI  + '" & ChrW(20182) & "'     END   'SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI',     MAIN.GOKEI_GK FROM( SELECT SUB1.SEIKYU_YM, SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,        COUNT(SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS KENSU,        MIN(SUB1.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD) AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,        SUM(SUB1.GOKEI_GK) AS GOKEI_GK  FROM   (SELECT T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_YM,       T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,        T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,        T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,        T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,        SUM(SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK) AS GOKEI_GK  FROM T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU  WHERE T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD like '1'  AND  T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.DELETE_FLG != '1'  GROUP BY T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_YM,T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,       T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,       T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,       T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS SUB1   GROUP BY SUB1.SEIKYU_YM, SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS MAIN, M_SOSHIKI,M_HIYO_KOMOKU  WHERE  MAIN.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD  AND   MAIN.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "Select DISTINCT T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM AS SEIKYU_YM, T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD, T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD, T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD AS SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD, T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD AS HIYOKOMOKU_CD, M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI AS HIYOKOMOKU_MEI, MOTO.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS MOTO_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI, SAKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.MEISAI_TESURYO_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.MEISAI_TOTAL_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.MEISAI_SHOHIZEI_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.HIYOKOMOKU_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SHOHIZEI_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.TESURYO_GK, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.TESURYO_RT, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SHOHIZEI_KBN, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.HASEI_DT, T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.BIKO FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI INNER JOIN T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU ON T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = T_SEISAN_SONOTA_HIYOU.SEIKYU_YM LEFT OUTER  Join M_HIYO_KOMOKU ON T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD LEFT  OUTER JOIN M_SOSHIKI MOTO ON T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD LEFT OUTER JOIN M_SOSHIKI SAKI ON T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD WHERE           (T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = '{0}') AND (T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = '{1}') AND (T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = '{2}') AND (T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '{3}') AND (T_SEISAN_MEISAI.HIYOKOMOKU_CD = '{4}')"

HIYOKOMOKU_CD = '{2}') SUB12,(SELECT MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD," & vbTab & "SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD," & vbTab & "SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD," & vbTab & "HIYOKOMOKU_CD," & vbTab & "COUNT(SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD) AS CNT," & vbTab & "MIN(HASEI_DT) AS HASEI_DT," & vbTab & "MIN(SHOHIZEI_KBN) AS SHOHIZEI_KBN," & vbTab & "MIN(SHOHIZEI_RT) AS SHOHIZEI_RT," & vbTab & "MIN(SYOSAI_TRI_MEI) AS SYOSAI_TRI_MEI," & vbTab & "MIN(SYOSAI_BIKO) AS SYOSAI_BIKO," & vbTab & "MIN(SYOSAI_AITE_MEI) AS SYOSAI_AITE_MEI," & vbTab & "MIN(SYOSAI_GK) AS SYOSAI_GK," & vbTab & "MIN(SYOSAI_ZAN_SU) AS SYOSAI_ZAN_SU," & vbTab & "MIN(UPDATE_DT) AS UPDATE_DT," & vbTab & "MIN(UPDATE_TNT_ID) AS UPDATE_TNT_ID," & vbTab & "MIN(GAMEN_ID) AS GAMEN_ID," & vbTab & "MIN(DELETE_FLG) AS DELETE_FLG  FROM T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU  WHERE SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'  AND  MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = '{1}'  AND  SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1'  AND  HIYOKOMOKU_CD = '{2}' GROUP BY MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD," & vbTab & "SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD," & vbTab & "SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD," & vbTab & "HIYOKOMOKU_CD) SUB0 WHERE MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB1.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB2.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB3.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB4.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB5.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB6.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB7.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB8.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB9.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB10.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB11.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB12.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD   AND MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB0.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD GROUP BY MAIN.SOSHIKI_CD,       MAIN.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,       SUB0.HASEI_DT,       SUB0.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,       SUB0.SHOHIZEI_KBN,       SUB0.SHOHIZEI_RT,       SUB0.SYOSAI_TRI_MEI,       SUB0.SYOSAI_BIKO,      SUB0.SYOSAI_AITE_MEI,       SUB0.SYOSAI_GK,       SUB0.SYOSAI_ZAN_SU,       SUB0.UPDATE_DT,       SUB0.UPDATE_TNT_ID,       SUB0.GAMEN_ID,       SUB0.DELETE_FLG,       SUB1.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB2.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB3.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB4.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB5.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB6.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB7.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB8.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB9.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB10.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB11.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB12.SEIKYU_GK,       SUB1.SHOHIZEI_GK,       SUB2.SHOHIZEI_GK,       SUB3.SHOHIZEI_GK,       SUB4.SHOHIZEI_GK, ' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function SEF0510() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "SELECT  MAIN.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_MEI,MAIN.KENSU,MAIN.SHOHIZEI_KBN,MAIN.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI + '" & ChrW(20182) & "' AS SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,MAIN.GOKEI_GK FROM(SELECT  SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,COUNT(SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS KENSU,MIN(SUB1.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD) AS SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,MAX(SUB1.SHOHIZEI_KBN) AS SHOHIZEI_KBN,SUM(SUB1.GOKEI_GK) AS GOKEI_GK FROM (SELECT  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SHOHIZEI_KBN,SUM(SEIKYU_GK + SHOHIZEI_GK) AS GOKEI_GK FROM T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU WHERE T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%' AND  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = '{1}' AND  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD LIKE '{2}%' AND  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1' AND  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.DELETE_FLG != '1' GROUP BY T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.SHOHIZEI_KBN,  T_SEISAN_TEIGAKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS SUB1 GROUP BY SUB1.HIYOKOMOKU_CD) AS MAIN,M_SOSHIKI,M_HIYO_KOMOKU WHERE  MAIN.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD  AND  MAIN.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

AND C.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD  AND C.UKETSUKE_NO = T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO.UKETSUKE_NO  AND T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1'  AND T_SEISAN_CRT_TESURYO.DELETE_FLG != 1) AS SUB  WHERE MAIN.SEIKYU_YM *= SUB.SEIKYU_YM      AND MAIN.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD      AND MAIN.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SUB.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD      AND MAIN.UKETSUKE_NO *= SUB.UKETSUKE_NO ) AS MAIN2  WHERE MAIN2.CRT_KOKYAKU_SEIKYU_GK = 0"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

      " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "JUCHU.SEIKYU_GK + JUCHU.SEIKYU_UTIZEI_GK + JUCHU.TATEKAE_GK + JUCHU.SHOHIZEI_GK AS GOUKEI,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "'1' AS SEQ_NO,                   " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "'4'" & vbTab & "AS SEIKYU_GK_KBN                   " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "FROM T_SEISAN_MEISAI,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "T_SEISAN_JUCHU AS JUCHU,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & vbTab & "T_JUCHU_KIHON                               WHERE T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM LIKE '{0}%'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{1}%'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '2'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KAKUTEI_KESHI_KBN = '0'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.DELETE_FLG = '0'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MEISAI_KBN = '2'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = '1'                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_YM = JUCHU.SEIKYU_YM                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = JUCHU.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD = JUCHU.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD = JUCHU.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = JUCHU.UKETSUKE_NO                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.SEIKYU_GK_KBN = JUCHU.SEIKYU_GK_KBN                             AND T_SEISAN_MEISAI.KANRI_NO = JUCHU.UKETSUKE_NO                             AND JUCHU.UKETSUKE_NO = T_JUCHU_KIHON.UKETSUKE_NO                                 AND   (JUCHU.SEIKYU_GK_KBN = '3' AND T_JUCHU_KIHON.KESSAI_KBN = '1')                    " & vbTab & vbTab & ") AS MAIN                   " & vbTab & vbTab & ") AS MAIN2,M_SOSHIKI AS MOTO,M_SOSHIKI AS SAKI                              WHERE MAIN2.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD = MOTO.SOSHIKI_CD                          AND     MAIN2.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD *= SAKI.SOSHIKI_CD                " & vbTab & vbTab & ") AS MAIN3,M_HIYO_KOMOKU                             WHERE MAIN3.HIYOKOMOKU_CD *= M_HIYO_KOMOKU.HIYOKOMOKU_CD                " & vbTab & "ORDER BY                   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.SEIKYU_YM,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.MOTO_SOSHIKI_CD,                   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.SAKI_SOSHIKI_CD,                   " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.SEIKYU_SIHARAI_CD,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.HIYOKOMOKU_CD,                    " & vbTab & vbTab & "MAIN3.SEQ_NO"
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "SELECT B.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI AS SOSHIKI_MEI, A.SHIHARAI_GOKEI_GK AS SHIHARAI_GOKEI_GK, A.SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK AS SEIKYU_GOKEI_GK FROM" & vbTab & "T_SEISAN_SOUSAI AS A INNER JOIN" & vbTab & "M_SOSHIKI  AS B ON B.SOSHIKI_CD = A.SOSHIKI_CD WHERE" & vbTab & "A.DELETE_FLG" & vbTab & "= 0 AND" & vbTab & "A.SEIKYU_YM" & vbTab & vbTab & "= '{0}' AND" & vbTab & "A.SOSHIKI_CD" & vbTab & "LIKE '{1}%' ORDER BY B.SOSHIKI_CD "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)

	End Try
	Return result
End Function

' Hato.DataAccess.MasterSQL
Public Function SMF0010() As String
	Dim result As String
	Try
		result = "SELECT M_USER_KANRI.USER_ID, M_USER_KANRI.PASSWORD,        M_USER_KANRI.SECURITY_CD, M_USER_KANRI.SOSHIKI_CD,         M_USER_KANRI.LOGIN_MEI, M_USER_KANRI.TANTOSHA_CD,        M_USER_KANRI.UPDATE_DT, M_USER_KANRI.UPDATE_TNT_ID,        M_USER_KANRI.GAMEN_ID, M_USER_KANRI.SIYO_FUKA_FLG,        isnull(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') as SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,        isnull(M_TANTOSHA.SHAIN_RYAKU_MEI,'') as SHAIN_RYAKU_MEI FROM   M_USER_KANRI,M_SOSHIKI,M_TANTOSHA WHERE  M_USER_KANRI.DELETE_FLG != 1  AND    M_USER_KANRI.SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD AND    M_USER_KANRI.TANTOSHA_CD *= M_TANTOSHA.TANTOSHA_CD ORDER BY M_USER_KANRI.USER_ID "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
		ProjectData.SetProjectError(expr_0C)
		Dim ex As Exception = expr_0C
		Throw ex
	End Try
	Return result
End Function

M_HOJIN.JIKAN_UNCHIN_CD,M_HOJIN.KYORI_UNCHIN_CD,              M_HOJIN.KAIAGE_PTN_CD_IPN,M_HOJIN.LEASE_PTN_CD_IPN,              M_HOJIN.KAIAGE_PTN_CD_JIM,M_HOJIN.LEASE_PTN_CD_JIM,              M_HOJIN.JISHA_MEI_OUT_KBN,M_HOJIN.JISHA_HOJIN_CD,               M_HOJIN.SOSHIKI_CD,M_HOJIN.EIGYO_TNT_CD,              M_HOJIN.SHIME_DT,M_HOJIN.UKETORI_TESURYO_KBN,M_HOJIN.UKETORI_TESURYO_RT,              M_HOJIN.SHIHARAI_TESURYO_KBN,M_HOJIN.SHIHARAI_TESURYO_RT,              M_HOJIN.UPDATE_DT,M_HOJIN.UPDATE_TNT_ID,              M_HOJIN.GAMEN_ID,M_HOJIN.DELETE_FLG,               M_HOJIN.GAMEN_ID,M_HOJIN.HIYOU_FUTAN_XML,              isnull(M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,'') as SOSHIKI_RYAKU_MEI,              '' as KAIAGE_MEI_IPN,              '' as LEASE_MEI_IPN,              '' as KAIAGE_MEI_JIM,              '' as LEASE_MEI_JIM,              '' as JIKAN_UNCHIN_MEI,              '' as KYORI_UNCHIN_MEI,              isnull(M_TANTOSHA.SHAIN_MEI,'') as EIGYO_TNT_MEI,              isnull(M_TANTOSHA.SHAIN_RYAKU_MEI,'') as EIGYO_TNT_RYAKU_MEI             FROM M_HOJIN,                  M_SOSHIKI,                   (SELECT TANTOSHA_CD,SHAIN_MEI,SHAIN_RYAKU_MEI FROM M_TANTOSHA WHERE SOSHIKI_CD  LIKE '{3}%'                          GROUP BY TANTOSHA_CD,SHAIN_MEI,SHAIN_RYAKU_MEI) AS M_TANTOSHA        WHERE M_HOJIN.HOJIN_CD LIKE '{0}%'        AND  M_HOJIN.HOJIN_MEI LIKE '{1}%' AND  M_HOJIN.HOJIN_KANA_MEI LIKE '{2}%'       AND  M_HOJIN.SOSHIKI_CD LIKE '{3}%' AND M_HOJIN.DELETE_FLG != 1       AND  M_HOJIN.SOSHIKI_CD *= M_SOSHIKI.SOSHIKI_CD        AND  M_HOJIN.EIGYO_TNT_CD *= M_TANTOSHA.TANTOSHA_CD        ORDER BY M_HOJIN.HOJIN_CD "
	Catch expr_0C As Exception
